Regenerate this file instead of editing it by hand.

```bash

tools/compiler_inventory.py --check docs/compiler/generated/reference.md
```

## Parser LL Status Words

| Word | Field | Meaning |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `0` | `accepted` | `nonzero when LL/HIR construction accepted the stream` |
| `1` | `error_pos` | `token position used as the primary syntax-error location` |
| `2` | `error_code` | `parser status code emitted by shader/table logic` |
| `3` | `detail` | `status-specific detail word` |
| `4` | `steps` | `LL/action step count` |
| `5` | `emit_len` | `production/HIR emission length used for active capacity` |
